				add_ownership={
					country={
						country="c:MEX"
						levels=1
					}
				}
				reserves=1
				activate_production_methods={ "pm_bleached_paper" "pm_rotary_valve_engine_building_paper_mill" }
			}
			create_building={
				building="building_naval_base"
				add_ownership={
					country={
						country="c:MEX"
						levels=2
					}
				}
				reserves=1
				activate_production_methods={ "pm_power_of_the_purse" }
			}
		}
	}
}
